              ifOperation: (MOD_EQUALS_0), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(30)
                characterSfx: s32'SE_BTL_BED_KAKUSEI_05'
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            if: Mem(ObjReg5)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(0)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
              checkDisplayedMesh: (PLAYER), s32'Bedw_matress'
              if: Mem(Tmp)
                createArgFromSocket: s32'chest', 0, 3
                createParticleWithArg2: s32'bed_501_buff_eyeaura_end', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
              else: 
                exPointFReset: (PLAYER), 0, 250000
                createParticle: s32'bed_501_buff_eyeaura', (EX_POINT_F)
              endElse: 
            endIf: 
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValue: Mem(ExGauge2), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
  endElse: 
  ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
    if: Mem(ExGauge3)
      if: Mem(BattleDoing)
        ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
          ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
            modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ExGauge3), Val(1)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge3), Val(11)
        bonePosition: s32'ex0', 0, 0, 0, 0, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0
        bonePosition: s32'ex1', 0, 0, 0, 0, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0
        boneRotation: s32'ex0', 0, 0, 0, 0, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0
        boneScale: s32'ex0', 1000, 1000, 1000, 0, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0
        boneScale: s32'ex1', 1000, 1000, 1000, 0, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0
        boneScale: s32'ex2', 1000, 1000, 1000, 0, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(1)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_1'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(2)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_1'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(3)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_2'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(4)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_2'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(5)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_3'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(6)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_3'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(7)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_3'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(10)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_1'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(20)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_1'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge4), Val(30)
        callSubroutine: s32'BoneControl_2'
      endIf:

        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge4), Val(0)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(ObjReg4)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1000)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)

        setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 0, 2
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1022)

        setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 1000, 2
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1034)
        setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 0, 2
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1038)
        setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 1000, 2
      endIf:

      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1100)

      endIf:

  if: Mem(Afro)
    ifNotInObject: (STACK0), Mem(ObjReg6)
      runOnObject: (STACK0)
        displayMesh: s32'Head_low_hair', 0
        displayMesh: s32'FAU_afro_low', 1
        overwriteLinkBone: s32'FAU_afro_low', s32'G_Head_def', s32'body', s32'G_Head_Attach'

        callPrivateFunction: s32'ans_ScarfUpdate', 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0
      endRunOnObject:

  endElse:

    endElse: 
  endIf:

beginSubroutine: s32'BED_ThrowEnemyCheck'
  upon: (ATTACK_COLLISION_MAIN_PLAYER)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (ATTACK_COLLISION_MAIN_PLAYER)
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'sol'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'kyk'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(2)
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'may'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(3)
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'axl'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(4)
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'chp'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(5)
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(6)
    endIf:

beginSubroutine: s32'CountDown_Controller'
  if: Mem(FuncArg1)
    storeValue: Mem(ExGauge1), Mem(FuncArg1)
    checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Ultimate1_Land'
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Ultimate1_Air'
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(1)
            runOnObject: (STACK0)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
            endRunOnObject: 
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(2)
            ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (STACK0), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
              checkCurrentStateName: (STACK0), s32'Delilah_AirEscape_After'
              ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
                runOnObject: (STACK0)
                  jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
                endRunOnObject: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(3)
            runOnObject: (STACK0)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
            endRunOnObject: 
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(4)
            ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (STACK0), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
              checkCurrentStateName: (STACK0), s32'Delilah_AirEscape_After'
              ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
                runOnObject: (STACK0)
                  jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
                endRunOnObject: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(5)
            runOnObject: (STACK0)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
            endRunOnObject: 
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(6)
            runOnObject: (STACK0)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
            endRunOnObject: 
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(7)
            runOnObject: (STACK0)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
            endRunOnObject: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    deactivateObjectByName: s32'count_down_timer'
    createObjectWithArg: s32'count_down_timer', (PLAYER)
    deactivateObjectByName: s32'count_down_parts'
    createObjectWithArg: s32'count_down_parts', (PLAYER)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(ExGauge1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg2), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(FuncArg0)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg2), Val(2)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(FuncArg0)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(FuncArg3)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(FuncArg3)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(FuncArg3)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(10)
      modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(10)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(ExGauge2)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(10)
      modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(10)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:
